[19/01/19, 6:44:10â€¯PM] â€ª+91Â 95919Â 89838â€¬: Hi all.... I need some advice please.  In the event of a NRI selling his property, there is a 20% TDS to be deducted by buyer and deposited on behalf of seller. However, if buyer is taking a 90% home loan, how will this deduction happen.
[19/01/19, 6:56:51â€¯PM] ~â€¯Prudent Estate: Better consultant with CA
[19/01/19, 6:58:29â€¯PM] ~â€¯Roof 360 Real Estate and Properties: Dear Mr. Romit. 
If the property is above 1Cr there will be surcharge of 15% or 10% if the property is below 1cr on the 20% tax for this type of transactions. The buyer has to apply for TAN if the property is above 50 Lakhs in order to pay the 20% tax behalf of the seller.
It's better to talk to the financial institution who is funding the property. It's better to workout a plan based on the sale agreement and the funding from the financial institution. For further info please consult a CA. 


This is something which is according to my knowledge, Dear Associates please share your opinions.
[19/01/19, 7:04:42â€¯PM] Amit Bannerjee-Ascat: BRH Agent: Which bank is funding 90 percent home loan. How I understand is own contribution which is around the TDS amount can be deposited as advance tax paid.

Mostly bank do make a payment (equal to the excess amount  like 10% in your case) to buyer also ...bank will bring 2 DD at the time of registration one for sellor and one for buyer. However you can addvise your sellor to apply and get a lower deduction certificate (LDC) from IT Deptt office. It is very fast nowadays ..you can get in 10-15 days. It will bring down TDS and the sellor donâ€™t have to wait for refund next year.

Local station to be informed with copy of passport and visa stamping along with permanent address from origin country.

Local station will inform FRRO 

Take supporting documents like work visa and company offer or appointment letter etc and do all transactions on cheque only from that person's account. 

Develop all communication in mail only. 

Generally anyone coming on work visa will have FRRO attestation and they need to be default in loop and work permit will be stamped by FRRO.

Seek a good advocate help for rental drafting etc is my suggestion besides these.
